I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `0.062258070344434831*A*log(0.9423435234237035*t + 1) - 0.13625696690019862*A`

This simplifies to: `A * [c_a + c_b * log(c_c * t + 1)]` where the entire expression is proportional to A, with a linear term in A and a term `A*log(c*t + 1)`.

Key structural features of GT:
- Every term is proportional to A (no standalone constants, no terms independent of A)
- Two basis functions: A and A*log(c*t + 1)
- No other variables or functions

Let me analyze each candidate:

This is exactly `A*(c0 + c1*log(c2*t + 1))`. Set c0 = -0.13626, c1 = 0.06226, c2 = 0.9423. **Perfect match.**
Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]

= `A*(c0+c1) + A*c2*log(c3*t+1)`. Same structure as GT with c0+c1 playing the role of the constant. **Match.**

= `A/(c1+t) * [c0*t + c2*log(c3*t+1) + c4 + c5*t*log(c3*t+1)]`
For this to equal `A*(a + b*log(d*t+1))`, we need `(c1+t)` to cancel. The expression has `t*log(...)/(c1+t)` which can't simplify to `log(...)` for all t. Let me check: if c5=0, we get `A/(c1+t)*[c0*t + c2*log(c3*t+1) + c4]`. For this to equal `A*(a + b*log(d*t+1))`, we need `(c0*t+c4)/(c1+t)` to be constant, which requires c0*t+c4 = k*(c1+t), so c4=k*c1, c0=k. Then we get `A*k + A*c2*log(c3*t+1)/(c1+t)`. The log term still has `1/(c1+t)` which can't be eliminated. Unless c2=0, but then we lose the log. **No match.**
